 ab ek baar phir se team india ko test main number ek banane kii jimmedaari yuva captain viraat kohli ke kandhon par hai
 Former captain Kapil Dev said that like Dhoni, Virat Kohli is also captaining well
 donon hi apana sau fisadi dete hai
 Dhoni has commanded the Test team of Team India for many years
 lekin ab unke test cricket se sanyas lene ke baad har kisi kii nigahen kohli par hai
 How they advance Team India
 kapil ne kaha ki 'vaise to dhoni or kohli kii soch main din or raat kaa antar he, or donon ne hi team ko jeet dilaane or number ek team banane main kisi tarah kii koi kami nahin chodi
 But Dhoni and Kohli have one thing in common that they give their 100% to win every Test match
 'aswin kaa rahaa he behtareen pradarshnahaal hi main khele gaye test muqablon main bhartiya spinner aar aswin kaa behtareen pradarshan rahaa he
 He has performed tremendously with the ball and bat
 westeindies ke khilaaf test siries main aswin main of da siries bhi rahe the
 He is also the highest wicket taker for Team India in the current period
 aswin test cricket main abtak chaar shatak bhi jade hai
 Which is equivalent to Team India opener Shikhar Dhawan
 purv captain kapil dev ne kaha ki 'jab se aswin ne bhartiya team main kadam rakhaa
 Since then, his performance has been spectacular
 maine kabhi sochaa bhi nahin tha ki itnaa aage jaaenge
 Harbhajan Singh was bowling brilliantly in the Indian team
 wo charsau wicket bhi hasil kar chuke the
 But then suddenly Ashwin started picking runs along with taking wickets
 mujhe lagata he ki aswin ek team india ke sabase ahm khilaadi hai'green park main milegi terning wicketnujiland ke khilaaf hone vaale 500wein aitihaasik test match main ummid kii ja rahi he ki, kiwi ballebaajon kaa swaagat spinneron ko madad karne vaali wicket se hoga
 The first match is going to be very important for the Indian team
 team india ke up-captain ajinkya rahane kaa maananaa he ki 'bharat ko apni dharti par 13 test match khilne hai
 In such a situation, the first Test match will be very important to achieve Momentum
 kisi siries kaa pehla test match kaaphi mahatvapurn hota he
 Kapil gives victory to Team India Kapil Dev has given the mantra of victory to Team India
 He has said that 'team India players should enjoy the brand of cricket and win the spectacular cricket game
 
 kyonki is mukaable kaa pareenam teen, chaar, yaa phir paanch din main nikal aayega or 500wein aitihaasik test match main jeet hasil karnaa khilaadiyon ke liye behad hi yaadgaar or anokhaa ahsaas hoga
 ' uttar pradesh main badhate aparaadh jahaan ek taraf rajya sarkaar ke liye badi chunauti ban gaya he, vahiin ek gaanv yahaan aisa bhi he, jahaan kalyug main 'ramraj' sthapit he
 No crime has been committed in this village even after six decades of independence
 ham baat kar rahe hai bahera gaanv kii jo uttar pradesh ke naksal prabhavit sonbhadra jile main he
 Since independence, till date there has been no criminal incident like assault, criminal, theft, robbery, kidnapping or murder
 aparaadh-mukt hone kaa daawa keval 700 kii aabaadi vaale bahera gaanv ke log hi kar rahe hai, aisa nahin he
 Police records also confirm his claims
 rampur bakonia thane ke record main yah gaanv aazaadee ke samay se lekar ab tak bilkul bedaag he
 Senior Superintendent of Police of the district, Subhash Chandra Dubey, says that despite being surrounded by Naxalites, not having a single FIR lodged in this village is a matter of great pleasure
 dube ke mutabik, pichhadaa hone hone ke baavjood bahera gaanv vastav main ek adarsh gaanv he
 The people of this village have set an example in front of the world
 bahera gaanv bhale hi varsho se aparaadh-mukt rahaa ho, lekin aisa nahin he ki duusare gaanvon kii tarah yahaan ke logon main aapasi manmutav nahin hota he
 Even if there is an estrangement between someone, the elders and the panchayat of the village resolve the matter within the border of the village, that is, there is no need to go to the police station and write a report
 ek gramin laalamani ne kaha, "duusare gaanv kii tarah hamaare gaanv main bhi logon ke bich manmutav hota he, lekin ham maamle ko lekar thane par na jaakar gaanv ke bade-burjugon ke paas mudda rakhte hai
 The elders who decide, both sides happily accept it
 "tippaniyan Another villager Siyaram said, "our village has got a distinct identity in the surrounding area due to the respect and trust of the elders
 " The Brahmin and Kshatriya fraternity comprises 30 per cent of the population of Bahera village, about 50 km from Sonbhadra city
 70 pratishat aabaadi dalit evam anya jatiyon kii he
 Most of the people in the village do farming and many households have jobs in government and private companies

 "tippaniyan Another villager Siyaram said, "our village has got a distinct identity in the surrounding area due to the respect and trust of the elders
 " The Brahmin and Kshatriya fraternity comprises 30 per cent of the population of Bahera village, about 50 km from Sonbhadra city
 70 pratishat aabaadi dalit evam anya jatiyon kii he
 Most of the people in the village do farming and many households have jobs in government and private companies
 jile ke varisht police adheekshak subhash chandra dube kaa kahana he ki naksaliyon se ghire hone ke baavjood is gaanv main ek bhi praathmiki darj na hona kaaphi khushi kii baat he
 According to Dubey, despite being backward, Bahera village is indeed an ideal village
 is gaanv ke logon ne duniya ke saamne ek misaal kaayam kii he
 Behera village may have been crime-free for years, but it is not that people like other villages do not have mutual estrangement
 agar kabhi kisi ke bich manmutav ho bhi gaya to gaanv ke bade-bujurg or panchayat, gaanv kii sarhad ke andar hi maamla sulajhza dete hai yani thane jaakar report likhavane kii naubat nahin aati
 Lalmani, a villager, said, "like other villages, there is rift among people in our village too, but we do not go to the police station and raise the issue with the elders of the village
 bade-bujurg jo faisla karte hai, donon paksh khushi-khushi use sweekaar kar lete hai
 "comments ek anya gramin siyaaraam ne kaha, "bade-bujurgon kaa sammaan or unke prati bharosa jataae jane ke kaaran aas-paas ke ilaake main hamaare gaanv ko vishisht pahchaan mili he
 " sonbhadra shahar se kareeb 50 kilometre dur bahera gaanv kii aabaadi kaa 30 pratishat hissaa brahman or kshatriya birdari kaa he
 Dalits and other castes constitute 70 percent of the population
 gaanv ke zyaadaatar log kheti karte hai or kai gharon ke log sarkari va nijee companiyon kii naukariyon main hai
